1. (ing. 1)

samebis kurTxeva

misi gegma

  1. qeba maradJams RmerT mamas
    da mis Zes qristes,
    marad dideba wmida suls _
    sams rogorc erTs!
  2. rodesac qmnilebas vumzerT,
    Cinebuls, diads,
    Cveni gulebi giZRvnian,
    Sen didebas!
  3. magram, RmerTo, Sen gwadia
    Zeebi gyavdes,
    visac uyvarxar Sens ZeSi
    da Sen gaqebs.
  4. saidumlo Seni gulis
    Cven gagvixseni,
    rom mogego Cveni guli
    siyvaruliT!
  5. qristes gamosyidviT sZlie
    borotis Zalebs!
    axal qmnilebaSi Cven dRes
    Tayvans gcemT Sen!
  6. qeba maradJams RmerT mamas
    da mis Zes qristes,
    marad dideba suls _
    sams rogorc erTs!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    2. (ing. 5)

    samebis kurTxeva

    misi mamoba

  1. RmerTo mama, Tayvans gcemT Sen!
    gakurTxebT Seni Svilni!
    Sen winaSe ubiwoni
    varT qristeSi rCeulni.
    Tayvans gcemT Sen! Tayvans gcemT Sen!
    abba, mama, gadidebT!
    Tayvans gcemT Sen! Tayvans gcemT Sen!
    abba, mama, gadidebT!
  2. maradiulo Zev, kravo,
    Tayvans gcemT mowiwebiT!
    RmerTis kravo, SeniTa varT
    RmerTTan dabrunebulni!
    geTayvanebiT, RmerTis Zev,
    romelic mokvdi CvenTvis!
    geTayvanebiT, RmerTis Zev,
    romelic mokvdi CvenTvis!
  3. mamav, Zev, da, wmida sulo,
    gadidebT sams rogorc erTs!
    aRgivlenT didebas gulSi,
    imisTvis, rasac gvaZlev!
    Tayvans gcemT Sen! Tayvans gcemT Sen!
    gakurTxebT maradis Sen!
    Tayvans gcemT Sen! Tayvans gcemT Sen!
    gakurTxebT maradis Sen!

  1. wmidav, wmidav, wmidav! o, RmerTo Zliero!

    6. (ing. 10)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    rogorc maradiulis

  1. o RmerTo, mamav marado,
    Sen xar xelTuqmneli `me var~!
    ZvelTa xar Sen uZvelesi,
    da upirvelesi JamTa!
  2. maradisagan xar RmerTi,
    aRematebi sivrces, dros!
    maradisobis sisavsev,
    usawyiso, usasrulo!
  3. marad xar wyaro yvelafris,
    zecaTa dafuZnebamde!
    upirvelesTa pirvel xar,
    mowinareTa winare!
  4. saukuno xar sicocxle,
    da arasodes mTavrdebi!
    yvelafris Semdegac Sen xar,
    warmavals aRematebi!
  5. Sena xar alfa, pirveli,
    boloc Sena xar, omega!
    srulyofileba, sisrule,
    xar TviTon unakloeba!
  6. gadidebT, maradiulo,
    vinaidan xar usazRvro!
    Sena xar ukidegano,
    srulyofileba unaklo!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    7. (ing. 11)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    rogorc sulis

  1. mamav, WeSmarito sulo,
    wmidao yvelaze;
    gixmobT WeSmaritebaSi
    da sulSi Tayvans gcemT!
  2. Sen suli gamogvisaxe,
    rom Cven Tayvani gceT,
    da sulis gamoZaxiliT
    vxdebiT erTsulad Cven.
  3. mama movida rogorc Ze,
    da Ze aris suli,
    raTa RmerTi Semovides
    Cvens sulSi viT madli.
  4. Ze saukuno sityvaa,
    da sityvaa suli;
    suli viT sicocxle modis,
    aaxlebs Cvens suls is!
  5. Seni suli Cvens sulSia,
    da am erTobaSi
    suli gvimowmebs Cvens sulTan,
    rom Cven Sengan viSviT.
  6. Seni suli migviZRveba,
    rom mudam gavyveT mas;
    sulierni vxdebiT da gvaqvs
    sicocxle, mSvidoba!
  7. yovelTvis sulSi gcemT Tayvans,
    sulSi mogmarTavT Sen,
    suls roca vaTavisuflebT,
    Sens saxebas vavlenT.
  8. mamav, Tayvans gcemT, radganac
    Sen axla suli xar;
    sulSi, WeSmaritebaSi
    aRgivlenT didebas.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    8. (ing. 12)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    rogorc sicocxlis saTavis

  1. sicocxlis wyaro xar, RmerTo,
    RvTaebrivi, uxvi!
    saukunod momdinare,
    sicocxlis nakadi!
  2. xalxs Soris moedinebi
    ZeSi, siyvarulSi;
    moedinebi viT suli,
    CvenSi Seni madliT.
  3. Tumca viyaviT Sors Sengan,
    codvaSi Caflulni,
    sicocxle, madli mogveci,
    nayidni varT ZeSi.
  4. Tumc xSirad ugulebelgyofT,
    Sens suls vanawyenebT,
    mainc modixar viT suli,
    gvaniWeb sicocxles.
  5. Sen rogorc suli Sens ZeSi
    xar CvenTan Serwymuli;
    urTierTobis wyalobiT
    gvcxeb Cven da izrdebi.
  6. RmerTis siyvaruls, qristes madls
    da sulis dinebas,
    mivyavarT Seni simdidriT
    maradis tkbobasTan.
  7. mama, Ze da wmida suli
    Cven Tavs gvevlebian;
    Sens siyvaruls erTad vumRerT,
    da gaqebT gulidan!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    9. (ing. 13)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    rogorc siyvarulis da sinaTlis

  1. ufalo, xar siyvaruli,
    sinaTle da sicocxle;
    sinaTles, siyvaruls avlen,
    ZeSi sicocxles gvaZlev.

    mis:
    ZeSi xar sicocxle,
    siyvarulo! sinaTlev!
    sinaTles, siyvaruls avlen,
    ZeSi sicocxles gvaZlev!

  1. siyvarulSi Sens arss vxedavT
    sinaTleSi _ Sens saqmeT;
    Sinagani siyvaruli
    Tan sdevs garegnul naTels.
  1. madlSi vxedavT Sens siyvaruls,
    naTelSi _ sinamdviles.
    siyvarulSi SeniT vtkbebiT,
    naTelSi SegicnobT Sen.
  2. siyvaruliT jvarze mokvdi,
    mogveci RvTis sicocxle;
    sinaTles moaqvs gageba,
    da Cven Sens sisxls viyenebT.
  3. siyvaruliT viT sicocxle
    gvaRwev da vurTierTobT;
    sinaTleSi vwmidandebiT,
    SenTan kavSirSi vcxovrobT.
  4. sinaTliT, gamwmendi sisxliT
    SevicnobT cxebulebas;
    Seni arsi _ siyvaruli
    CvenSi metad iRvreba.
  5. siyvaruliT gavxdiT Svilni,
    geZaxiT `abba mamas~;
    Suqi gafantavs Cvens wyvdiads,
    Zisebr Cvenc davinaxavT.

    mis:
    madlSi _ siyvaruli!
    naTelSi _ sinamdvile!
    saukunod gangadidebT,
    da SegicnobT marad Sen!



    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    10. (ing. 14)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi ukvdaveba

  1. ukvdavo, brZeno, uxilavo RmerTo,
    TvalTagan uwvdomel naTelSi myofo,
    dReebiT Zvelo da unetareso,
    qeba Sens saxels, Zliero, diado.
  2. mdumarev, Zliero, dauRalavo,
    dinjo da uzenaeso mmarTvelo,
    mTebiviT maRlaa Seni simarTle,
    Rrublad gmosavs siyvaruli, sikeTe.
  3. sicocxles aniWeb dids Tu pataras,
    da erTaderTi sicocxle Tavad xar;
    viT balaxi Cven vyvavilobT da vWknebiT,
    magram Sen arasodes ar icvlebi.
  4. didebis da sinaTlis RmerTo mama,
    Seni angelozebi gcemen Tayvans;
    Cvenc gadidebT Sen da gTxovT, dagvanaxve:
    rom sinaTlis brwyinvaleba gfaravs Sen!
  5. ukvdavo, brZeno, uxilavo RmerTo,
    TvalTagan uwvdomel naTelSi myofo,
    dReebiT Zvelo da unetareso,
    qeba Sens saxels, Zliero, diado.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    11. (ing. 15)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi aRmatebuloba

  1. RmerTo, Sena xar wmida,
    da aRmatebuli!
    Seudarebeli xar,
    da ara gyavs toli!
    wmidaTa uwmidesos
    samyaro geZaxis!
    Sens Zalas da bunebas
    daCrdilavs veravin!
  2. erTaderTi xar wmida,
    srulyofilo RmerTo;
    wmindaze ufro wmindav,
    marTalze marTalo;
    vervin gagitoldeba,
    mova SenTan axlos;
    veravin Caganacvlebs,
    da ver Seuracxgyofs.
  3. saucxoov, saCinov,
    mSvenieri Sen xar!
    rCeulTa umjobeso,
    vervin Segedreba.
    marTalT Soris marTalo,
    ubadlov sruliad;
    kacTa mSveneba Sensas
    ver gautoldeba!
  4. umaRlesi siwmide
    Sen Cven mogvimzade,
    Sens bunebas didebuls
    ukve veziareT.
    aRmatebuleba gvaqvs
    Cven Sens bunebaSi!
    sisavsemde vizrdebiT,
    wmida sicocxleSi!
  5. gadidebT da Tayvans gcemT,
    Seni siwmidisTvis,
    maRali bunebisTvis
    Cven erTxmad gimReriT.
    Sens bunebas ubadlos
    veziarebiT kvlav;
    gamogvyofs yvelafrisgan
    Cven Seni buneba.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    12. (ing. 16)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi siaxle

  1. mamav, viT maradmwvane, xar
    mudmivad axali!
    maradiulad cocxali,
    da qorfa namiviT!

    mis:
    mama, Sena xar ucvleli
    da uberebeli!
    uSreti wlebiT gvauwyeb,
    Sens siaxles, mudmivs!

  1. Sena xar RmerTi, `axali~,
    dauZvelebeli!
    da wlebis miuxedavad,
    qorfa xar da norCi!
  1. Sens mocemul kurTxevebSi
    Sens siaxles vxedavT,
    Seni gzebiviT axali
    aris Seni aRTqma!
  1. axal qmnilebad gvaqcie,
    axal suliT, guliT;
    dRiTi dRe vtovebT siZveles,
    da mudam vaxldebiT.
  1. axal casa da miwaze
    axal qalaqs vxedavT;
    yovel Tve axal nayofiT
    xalxi ikurneba.
  1. o mamav, marad axalo,
    SenSia siaxle;

    erTad gangadidebT.

    13. (ing. 17)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi sidiade

  1. mama RmerTo, roca qmnilebas vucqer,
    vxedav cis da miwis saocrebebs.
    yvelaferSi, didsa Tu pataraSi,
    Sens Zalas vxedav, didebuls, uTqmels.

    mis:
    mTeli arsebiT gimReriT qebas,
    saocaro! didebulo!
    maradiulad gimRereb qebas,
    saocaro! didebulo!

  1. rodesac vtkbebi gadarCenis madliT,
    da vfiqrob Sens warmogzavnil Zeze,
    vinc sikvdiliT Cven gvSva axal qmnilebad,
    visSic srulad vxedavT Sens sicocxles.
  2. eklesiis kurTxeul erTobaSi,
    yvela viziarebT Sens sicocxles.
    vSendebiT Sens didebul sacxovreblad,
    rom Seni gamovxatoT sisavse!
  3. velodebi momaval saukunes,
    axal ierusalimSi yofnas.
    axal zecasa da axal miwaze,
    gamoxatuli sruliad Sen xar.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    14. (ing. 18)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi erTguleba

  1. erTgulo da saimedo,
    Cemo RmerTo mama!
    Sens erTgulebas samyaro,
    aRiarebs erTxmad!

    mis:
    Tayvans gcem erTgulebisTvis,
    romelic mtkicea;
    is Sen caSi daafuZne,
    da dgas Cvens garantad!

  1. SenTan ar aris cvlilebis
    mciredi aCrdilic!
    Sen xar is, vinc iyo, aris,
    Sen marad iqnebi!
  1. Seni sityvebi SensaviT
    WeSmaritebaa!
    ca da miwa gardaxdeba,
    Seni sityva _ ara!
  1. Sen uangarod mogvixme
    da dagvasaCuqre.
    madli da wyaloba marad
    Sens saxelSi gvaqvs Cven!
  1. Seni sityva erTgulebiT
    Tavdebia Cemi;
    mis mier maqvs darwmuneba
    SenSi gadarCenis.
  1. maSinac ki, Tu orggulob,
    erTguli rCebi Sen;
    ar Ralatob sakuTar Tavs,
    Sens sityvas asruleb!
  1. Sens moxmobasa da aRTqmas
    srulqmni erTgulebiT;
    vRebulob Sens erTgulebas,
    vikvebebi SeniT.
  2. taxtis irgvliv cisartyela
    erTgulebas mowmobs;

    Tan sdevs saukunod!

    15. (ing. 19)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi erTguleba

  1. didad erTgulo, Cemo RmerTo mama,
    arasodes ar Seicvlebi Sen;
    Seni TanagrZnobebi mudam Tan msdevs,
    maradiulad igive xar Sen.

    mis:
    o ra erTguli xar! o ra erTguli xar!
    yovel diliT Sens wyalobebs vxedav.
    is, rac mWirdeba, Senma xelma momca;
    diadia Seni erTguleba!

  1. weliwadis oTxi dro, mze da mTvare,
    varskvlavebi rogorc cis mxedroba,
    mTeli buneba mravalmxrivi gzebiT,
    amtkicebs Sens diad erTgulebas.
  2. codvis patiebas, uryev mSvidobas,
    Sens Zvirfas Rimils da Semweobas;
    sicocxlis Zalas da momavlis imeds _
    vRebulob sxva uamrav kurTxevas!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    16. (ing. 20)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi samarTlianoba

  1. Cveno mama RmerTo, gaqebT
    samarTlianobisTvis;
    qristeSi Cven gagvamarTle,
    vin daTrgunavs Cvens sindiss?
    samarTliano, erTgulo,
    vdgavarT Sens simarTleze;
    usamarTloba verasdros
    cvlis Sens samarTlian xels.
  2. mamav yvela Cveni codva
    Sen dade iesoze;
    wmida rjulis moTxovnebi
    aRasrula Senma Zem.
    misiT rogorc msxverpliT srulad
    xom dakmayofildi Sen;
    rogorRa mogvTxov xelaxla
    SemogwiroT msxverpli Sen?
  3. RmerTo mamav, ieso Cvens
    Canacvlebad miiRe;
    marTals umarTloTa gamo
    Sen xom msjavri daade.
    Seni damtkicebis niSnad
    Sens marjvniv is daisvi;
    sruliad akmayofilebs
    Sens maRal moTxovnebs is.
  4. iesos sisxliT, mama, vflobT
    samarTlianobas Sens;
    Seni simarTliT daculebs
    veraferi Segvaryevs.
    gagvxade Cven Sens simarTled,
    msjavrs veravin ver dagvdebs;
    axal ierusalimSi
    sul amas davamowmebT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    17. (ing. 21)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi samarTlianoba

  1. gaqebT simarTlisTvis, mama;
    da Sens samarTlianobas
    mowmobad vatarebT.
    Sena xar samarTliani,
    Rirsi, rom kacobriobis
    iyo mosamarTle.
  2. mama, xar wmida, marTali,
    Seni taxtis saZirkveli
    Seni simarTlea.
    Seni simarTlis wyalobiT,
    mefobs qristes madli CvenSi
    da Cven gvaqvs mSvidoba.
  3. Seni samarTlianobiT
    Ze gaekra jvarze CvenTvis,
    amgvarad gviyide;
    roca Cven miviReT qriste,
    Sen namdvilad gagvamarTle,
    da gadagvarCine.
  4. Seni simarTlis wyalobiT
    Sen akurTxe patiebiT
    xalxebi Zvel droSi;
    Seni simarTle axlac Cans,
    codvilT patiob Sen kvlavac
    am saukuneSi.
  5. mamav, yvela xalxs im erT dRes
    gansji Seni simarTliT Sen
    Seni qriste ufliT;
    Cven ki kvlav vidgebiT mtkiced,
    Sens simarTles davamowmebT
    Cveni uflis madlSi.
  6. Sens samefoSi simarTle
    mSvidobas saZirkvlad udevs
    srul harmoniaSi.
    axal casa da miwaze,
    imefebs Seni simarTle,
    Sen mier aRTqmuli.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    18. (ing. 22)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi siwmide

  1. o wmida mama, Tayvans gcemT,
    pativiT gimReriT Sen;
    wmida da didebuli xar,
    Sens wmida saxels vaqebT.
  2. mosiyvarule xar guliT,
    gzebiT _ samarTliani;
    Seni bunebis siwmide
    Cven gveZleva qristeSi.
  3. Cveni uflis, qristes sisxliT
    maradis wmidagvyavi;
    Seni WeSmariti sityviT
    codvilni gamogvyavi.
  4. Seni wmida suliT gvqmeni
    SenTvis wmidad Cven yvela;
    Cveni samive nawili
    srulad ganiwmideba.
  5. iesos wmida sicocxle
    madliT gvaqvs miRebuli;
    TviT Seni wmida bunebis
    varT Cven moziareni.
  6. rodesac wmida qalaqSi
    Sens siwmides sruliad
    gaviziarebT maradis,
    ganvacxadebT: `wmida xar~.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    19. (ing. 23)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi sibrZne

  1. mama RmerTo, Sens sibrZneSi,
    Seni nebisamebr,
    Zem aavsos yvelaferi _
    es Sen ganizraxe.

    mis:
    Sens sibrZnes ukideganos
    vin SeZlebs, rom Cawvdes?
    magram madlsa da wyalobas,
    mamav, masSi gvaZlev!

  1. Sen brZnulad qmen yvelaferi,
    vin uwys Sens gonebas?
    Sengan, SeniT da Senken ars,
    yvelaferi, mamav.
  1. yvela codvaSi Caketa
    Senma sibrZnem, raTa
    ver viqadodeT verafriT
    RvTis wyalobis garda.
  1. Sens sibrZneSi gamosyidva
    jvarze aRasrule,
    rom Cvens sulSi Sen rogorc ganZs
    gqonoda savane.
  1. eklesiiT Sen auwyeb
    Sens sibrZnes mTavrobebs,
    Sens mravalmxriv sibrZnes CveniT
    zecani xedaven.
  1. Sens wyalobas ganvadidebT
    Cven wmida qalaqSi,
    saukunod gamJRavndeba
    Seni sibrZne CvenTvis.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    20. (ing. 24)

    mamis Tayvaniscema

    misi sibrZne

  1. o RmerTo, Seni sibrZne da
    madli qristeSia;
    is qmeni Sen CvenTvis sibrZned,
    masSi vxedavT Sens gzas.
  2. is madlis gzaa da masSi
    aris Seni gegma;

    135. (ing. 187)

    es himni imRereba xuTi sxvadasxva gziT:

    2. strofebi 1, 9-dan 13-mde, 26.

  16. cxvris farexi, rom davtovoT,

  17. gansabanlis meSveobiT,

  4. sikvdiliT codva waSale,
    zecad zixar, moeli
    yvela mtris damorCilebas,
    aRsrulebas RvTis nebis.
  5. saukeTeso saxeli,
    gaqvs RvTisgan naboZebi,
    RvTis Ze xar, sicocxle CvenTvis,
    axla xar myofi sulSi.
  6. samefo dgas simarTleze,
    uryevi gaqvs Sen taxti;
    RmerTma gcxo Sen siyvarulSi
    xar maradis ucvleli.
  7. WeSmaritad Sen xar kaci,
    Cvens bunebas srulad flob;
    madliT igeme sikvdili,
    raTa Sen dagemsgavsoT.
  8. Sen dideba gaqvs gvirgvinad
    yovelive gmorCilobs;
    gadarCenis winamZRolo,
    tanjvebiT srulyofilo.
  9. sikvdiliT mteri Semusre,
    Cvenc gagvaTavisufle;
    sicocxleSi gvawmidaneb,
    migviZRvi didebisken.
  10. Cven Soris xar, rogorc Sens Zmebs
    gvauwyeb mamis saxels;
    eklesiaSi himns mReri,
    CvenTan erTad RmerTs aqeb.
  11. Sen xar saxlis mSenebeli,
    moses aRematebi;
    mociquli RmerTisagan,
    Sen Rirsi xar didebis.
  12. mosvenebaSi SegyavarT,
    ieso naves Ze xar;
    Sen xar sruli gadarCena
    mxolod SenSi gvaqvs rwmena.
  13. RvTiuri xar mosveneba,
    axla Cvens sulSi mkvidrob;
    SevideT keTil miwaze,
    rom srulad dagimkvidroT.
  14. aarons aRematebi,
    Sen TviTon gaxdi msxverpli;
    mRvdelTmTavari xar, Sesuli
    cad wmidaTa wmidaSi.
  15. namdvili melqisedeki
    xar, sicocxlis momcemi;
    `pur-RviniT~ gvemsaxurebi,
    rogorc ki dagvWirdebi.
  16. Sen xar ukeTesi msxverpli,
    maradiuli suliT;
    Cven gamo RmerTs Seewire,
    gvaqvs Seni miRwevebi.
  17. Seni sisxliT ukeTesi
    aRTqma caSi daido;
    maTTvis, vinc gamoisyide,
    es aRTqmaa sarwmuno.
  18. axali aRTqmis avtoro,
    Sen gekuTvnis dideba;
    raTa uxvad dagimkvidroT,
    Cven mogveci es aRTqma.
  19. xar aRTqmis aRmsrulebeli,
    aRdgomis sicocxlis gziT;
    RvTis amorCevas asruleb
    Seni SuamdgomlobiT.
  20. axla Sen xar fardis miRma,
    iq pirveli Sexvedi;
    rom banaks gareT Cven erTad
    virbinoT RvTis sicocxliT.
  21. rwmenis damwyebo, srulmyofo,
    da damasrulebelo.
    siyvaruliTa da rwmeniT
    mogyvebiT da gmorCilobT.
  22. Seudarebeli aris
    CvenTvis Seni Rirseba;
    ar ZalgviZs, rom SevafasoT
    Seni srulyofileba.

    misma oqrom da vercxlma yvelas
    unaTos! unaTos!
    RmerT-kravi gaxda Cveni tkboba
    SigniT saukunod!

  5. qari, Rrubeli, cecxli, eleqtroni _
    CvenSi inergeba;
    dae mudmivad gagrZeldes es cikli
    sul metad, sul metad!

    ufalo, dagvbere, gvinaTe
    eufle Cvens arsebas,
    rom mogipovoT gamudmebiT
    Sens gamosaxatad.



    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    451. (ing. 1201)

  1. RvTis saxlidan CrdiloeTiT
    modis qari, grigali.
    Zlevamosili suli qris,
    Cvens arsebas CasZaxis.
    aRgvZravs siRrmeebisken is,
    gvaRviZebs es qari Cven!
    vexsnebiT samuSaos RvTis,
    Rrubeli modis Cvenze.
  2. uflis sitkbos, Tandaswrebas
    vpoulobT am RrubelSi;
    ar veyrdnobiT sakuTar Tavs,
    masze varT mindobilni.
    magram Rrubels cecxli moaqvs,
    STanTqavs Cvens `mes~, _ gulisTqmebs,
    rom gadagvaqcios ferflad,
    zeciurs is CvenSi debs.
  3. cecxlidan Cans eleqtroni,
    kaSkaSa da naTeli.
    Seerwynen RmerTi da kaci
    rogorc oqro da vercxli!
    o ufalo, krav-RmerTo, Sen
    xar es mnaTi metali.
    CvenSi metad Cainerge,
    rom Candes eleqtroni.
  4. cocxali arseba vxdebiT
    Cven am ciklis gavlisas,
    iesos mis sicocxleSi
    erTobiT gamovxatavT.
    mas gamovxatavT rogorc kacs,
    natifs, keTils, srulyofils;
    wesiersa da rigians,
    adamians RvTaebrivs.
  5. mas gamovxatavT rogorc loms,
    romelic Tvis mtrebs ipyrobs;
    is sul erTgulad msaxurobs,
    rogorc xari morCilobs.
    mas gamovxatavT viT arwivs,
    is maRlaa yvelaze;
    mas ver Seakavebs SiSi,
    dafrinavs marlobebze.
  6. RmerTis mier Cvenze Sroma
    moCans am suraTebSi!
    cecxls, Rrubels, eleqtrons da qars
    sdevs arseba cocxali:
    kaci, xari, lom-arwivi _
    oTxi saxe gveqneba,
    Tu ufals SevWamT yovelTvis,
    mas srulad gamovxatavT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    452. (ing. 622)

  1. Tu Cven aviRebT jvars, mxolod tanjva gvelis?
    ara, Tu vatarebT jvars, udaod vkvdebiT!
    jvris mniSvnelobaa viyoT daklulebi;
    `me~ jvarcmulia, Cven mier jvris gancdebiT.

    mxolod jvriT xdeba qriste sicocxle Cveni;
    roca vkvdebiT, qriste gamoixateba.
  3. jvris mizania RmerTis neba aRsruldes;
    am nebis mTavari mteri Cveni `mea~.
    magram Tu uarvyofT Cvens mSvinva sicocxles,
    RvTis neba aRsruldeba da ayvavdeba.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    453. (ing. 626)

  1. zeTisxili zeTad xdeba,

    Sen unda gandidde,

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    454. (ing. 628)

  1. gzas gavdivarT beTleemze,

  7. win miviwevT! Sors naTeba

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    457. (ing. 635)

  1. modiT SevxedoT, viswavloT

  2. araviTari dideba

  3. vazi Zelze mibmulia,

    sicocxlis sisavsidan.
    erTmaneTze gadawnuli
    mravali nazi toti,
    cis laJvardisken izrdeba,
    haeris sitkboebiT.
  5. roca modis mevenaxe,
    Tan moaqvs makrateli,
    rom SekriWos siamaye,
    aris daundobeli.
    ar zrunavs mis sinazeze,
    aramed zusti gasxvliT,
    aSorebs lamaz, zedmet rqebs,
    ase mohyavs wesrigSi.
  6. gana sakuTari Tavi
    ebraleba am dros vazs?
    piriqiT, metad exsneba,
    mas, vinc ase Rrmad daWra;
    silamaze moaSora,
    vazs, rom misi sicocxle,
    amaod ar gaixarjos
    da nayofebi hqondes.
  7. dRiTidRe Zlierdebian,
    sisxlmdinare totebi,
    toti, romelic mkvidrdeba,
    mtevnebs uxvad warmoqmnis.
    mcxunvare mzis qveS yofnisas,
    scviva xmeli foToli;
    ase, ufro meti moaqvs
    mas mwife mosavali.
  8. nayofiT datvirTul totebs,
    saxe miwisaken aqvT;
    Sromas moaqvs Sedegi Tu,
    tanjvebSi gavlilia.
    vazi nugeScemulia
    simwifis miRwevisas;
    Tumc krefis dro axlovdeba,
    kvlav wuxilis dRe dgeba.
  9. xeli dakrefs, fexi daWylets

    idens wiTel mdinared.
    minarevebis gareSe,
    sisxliviT wiTeli mosCqefs
    Tavisuflad, didebulad

  10. axla vazi garegnulad,
    uSnod, sacodavad Cans;
    yvelaferi gaiRo da
    bnelma Ramem moicva.
    arvin emadliereba,
    mxiaruli RvinisTvis;
    dgas daWrilad, unayofod
    sul erTicali Stambi.
  11. sitkbos inarCunebs Rvino
    zamTris ganmavlobaSi,
    yvelas, vinc sicivisgan TrTis
    uqrobs tkivils, SfoTs, wuxils.
    yvelasgan mitovebuli
    vazi yinva-TovlSi dgas;
    mtkiced umklavdeba tkivils,
    rTulia amis aRqma.
  12. zamTris miwuruls, vazi kvlav
    Tavidan emzadeba;
    yvavis, ezrdeba totebi,
    vazi isev mwvandeba.
    ar wuwunebs da arc Civis
    sastikad mopyrobaze,
    danakargis gamo ar surs
    misi ZRveni Semcirdes.
  13. sunTqavs haers, ciurs, sufTas,
    vazi, mxrebs imaRlebs kvlav,
    ver akavebs miwiuri,
    binZuri mRelvareba.
    RimiliT, msxverplad swiravs Tavs,
    siyvaruliT mzadaa;
    TiTqos arc gamoucdia
    aranairi tanjva.
  14. wveni, sisxli, Rvino modis
    vazis xis totebisgan.
    tanjvebisgan, rac man gavlo
    sacodavi gaxada?
    svaven da mxiaruloben
    loTebi da mwirebi;
    aseTi tkboba, garToba
    nuTu maT mdidrebs gaxdis?
  15. sicocxles zomavs zarali
    da ara SenaZeni;
    ramdens davlevT eg ki ara,
    Cvengan ramdens gadmovRvriT;
    siyvaruli gvaZlierebs,
    rom msxverpli vataroT Cven;
    vinac meti daiTmina,
    miT meti aqvs sxvas misces.
  16. vinc sakuTar Tavs ar indobs,
    RmerTi metad iyenebs;
    vinc tkivils ar uSindeba,
    sxvas tanjvisas amxnevebs.
    vinc ar icis tanjvis gemo,
    `JRaruna spilenZia~;
    vinc mSvinva sicocxle daTmo,
    tkbeba aRuwerelad.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    466. (ing. 659)

  1. ixareT ufalSi! man Segviwyala,

    aseT dros RmerTis winaSe locviT,
    uZlurebs suli gvexmareba.
  2. vloculob, ar gaaRrmavo tanjva,
    msurs gavTavisuflde me maTgan;
    dae, aRsruldes Seni neba da
    miRebul iqnas Tasi Sengan.
    mtkivneuli gansacdelebisas,
    gulSi mainc aris mSvidoba;
    yvela eWvi Sewyda, radgan gulSi
    RvTis siyvaruli CaiRvara.
  3. RmerTi awyobs yvelafers Cven irgvliv,
    misi yovlismpyrobeli xeliT;
    yvela pirovneba (Tumc ver vxedavT)
    Tanaxmadaa misi gegmis.
    yvela gansacdeli pasuxia,
    mlocveli sulisTvis mamisgan;
    man metad mogvipovos tanjvisas,
    veziaroT qristes didebas.
  4. is, vinc Tavisi Ze ar daindo,
    arc Cven agvaridebs gamwvrTnel xels;
    gana datovebs dausrulebels,
    brZeni meqoTne Tavis Sedevrs?
    RmerTis gulis survili aris, rom
    qristes mravali Zma Cven viyoT;
    qristea mamis pirmSo da mas surs,
    Cven, yvelani mas davemsgavsoT.
  5. RvTis memkvidreni varT! - o, dideba!
    da qristes Tanamemkvidreni;
    Tumc axlandeli tanjvebi gvTrgunavs,
    win aris didebis imedi!
    Cveni moyvarulis meSveobiT,
    varT mZlevelze metad Zlieri;
    mTeli qmnileba ucdis dRes,roca
    unda gamovlindnen RvTis Zeni.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    490. (ing. 733)

  1. edemis baRSi, ori xis
    win, RmerTma dasva adami,
    sicocxlis da Secnobis xe
    dgas RvTisa da satanisTvis
  2. sicocxlis xe aris centri
    RvTis maradiuli gegmis,
    RmerTia, rogorc sicocxle
    qristeSi yvela kacisTvis
  3. aris sxva wyaroc Secnobis
    gafrTxilebaa yvelasTvis,
    RmerTis gareT ars sxva wyaro _
    sikvdilis wyaro satanis
  4. Tu kaci sicocxlis xidan
    SeWams, gardaisaxeba,
    Zvirfas qvebad aSendeba
    RvTis mizani Sesruldeba.
  5. Tu Secnobis xes miiRebs,
    satana Seva am kacSi,
    rogorc codva, is mas moklavs,
    ver Seasrulebs RvTis gegmas.
  6. sicocxlis wyaro RmerTia
    Cveni sicocxle da sunTqva,
    sxva rames Tu SevexebiT
    wyaro sikvdili iqneba.
  7. mxolod codna sikvdilia,
    Tumc iyos cudi an kargi,
    damoukideblad RvTisgan,
    aris satanis nayofi
  8. ara mxolod cudi, kargic
    qristes winaaRmdeg aris;
    Secnobis xis nayofia
    sicocxlis winaaRmdegi
  9. ufalo, gvaswavle mxolod,
    Sen rom SegexoT yovel dros,
    ar SevexoT arc kargs, arc cuds
    Seni sicocxliT avivsoT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    491. (ing. 734)

  1. RvTis kanoni wmida, kargi
    iTxovs vakeToT sikeTe,
    mizani misi, gvaCvenos _
    ver vasrulebT RvTis moTxovnebs.
  2. gonebaSia kanoni,
    is cdilobs kargis keTebas,
    sxeulSi _ codvis kanoni
    mas imorCilebs yovel wams.
  3. gonebaSia kanoni _
    Tandayolili bunebiT,
    ufalma Seqmna is CvenSi
    saTanado qcevisaTvis.
  4. codvis kanons sxeulebSi
    satanisgan aqvs saTave,
    dacemisas cbierebiT
    SemoiWra, davemoneT.
  5. satanis kanoni aris,
    codvis kanoni sxeulSi;
    ufro Zlieri kanoni
    gonebaSi myof kanonze.
  6. Cvens sulSi aris kanoni,
    sicocxlis sulis kanoni,
    es aris RmerTis sicocxle,
    miviReT xelaxlaSobiT.
  7. sulis kanoni mZleveli
    aRemateba yvelafers,
    codvisgan gvaTavisuflebs,
    asrulebs RmerTis moTxovnebs.
  8. mudam movmarToT goneba,
    Cvens Rrma nawilSi, sulisken
    nu movmarTavT Cvens gonebas
    dacemuli xorcisaken.
  9. Tu ars goneba xorcisken
    iq sufevs codva, sikvdili,
    Tu ars goneba sulisken
    sicocxle, mSvidoba ari.
  10. es Tavisuflebis gzaa,
    es aris gza gamarjvebis,
    ufalo, sulSi gvacxovre
    viaroT erTad am sulSi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    492. (ing. 735)

  1. werilis rjuli RmerTs gvixsnis
    RvTis mowmobaa namdvili
    bunebiT RmerTi marTali
    mosiyvarule, wmidaa.
  2. misi bunebis Tanaxmad
    kanoni iTxovs icxovro,
    rom mSvinva Cveni gamarTldes,
    yvela kurTxeva miviRoT.
  3. sicocxles, rjuli ver gvaZlevs
    verc Zalas, momaragebas
    moTxovna misi marTali
    amxels Cvens ususurobas.
  4. rjulis micemis mizani,
    codvis mxilebisTvisaa,
    arRvevs mas, kaci gebulobs,
    rom codvas miyidulia.
  5. kanoni yvelas adumebs,
    codvis qveS aqcevs ra yvelas;
    RmerTis qristesTan mivyavarT
    vRebulobT masSi kurTxevas.
  6. kanoni winasaxea
    qristes, rogorc RvTis mowmobis
    gamoxatavs mis siyvaruls
    RvTis samarTals da siwmides.
  7. es, qristea RvTis mowmoba,
    sicocxliT rom gvamaragebs,
    raTa marTali moTxovna
    kanonis CvenSi aRsruldes.
  8. cocxali mowmobaa RvTis,
    mZlevel sicocxles gvaniWebs
    kanonisaTvis movkvdiT, rom
    mis sulSi nayofi gvqondes.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    493. (ing. 736)

  1. uwin qvaze iyo RmerTis
    kanoni amotvifruli;
    axla ki is Cvens gulebSi
    sicocxlis kanonad aris.
  2. aso gvavalebs sikeTes,
    da is amxels Cvens sisustes;
    sicocxle ki Zalas gvaZlevs,
    rom vasoamovnoT Cvens RmerTs.
  3. asos kanons CvenTvis moaqvs
    RmerTze garegnuli codna;
    sicocxlis kanons Sewevna
    moaqvs, Sinagani codna.
  4. asos kanons SeuZlia
    garedan mcnebebiT marTva;
    sicocxlis kanoni marTavs
    cocxali codniT Signidan.
  5. cocxali kanoni axla
    Rrmad moZraobs Cvens gancdebSi,
    gvaregulirebs Signidan,
    da gvaZlevs grZnobas Cven SigniT.
  6. is Cven Rrmad gvaregulirebs,
    Cveni arsebis wiaRSi,
    cocxal Semecnebas gvaZlevs,
    da nergavs TviT RmerTs Cven SigniT.
  7. arvisgan gvWirdeba swavla,
    Cven gvaqvs sicocxlis kanoni,
    misiT gvaqvs RmerTis Secnoba,
    is Sinaganad gvaswavlis.
  8. ufalo, gvaswavle, rom Cven
    misiT viaroT, vusminoT,
    rom vinZlo geziaroT Sen
    da cocxali gziT SegicnoT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    494. (ing. 737)

  1. marad sicocxles aqvs
    urTierToba;
    sulis ziareba
    gvixsnis brZolisgan.
  2. RvTiur ziarebas
    gvaZlevs sicocxle;
    ufal sulTan erTi
    ase vxdebiT Cven.
  3. is gvaZlevs Cven sulis
    urTierTobas;
    urTierTobas ki
    madli mohyveba.
  4. sicocxlis wyalobiT
    vurTierTobT Cven;
    naTelSi mivyavarT
    sulis dinebas.
  5. gawmenda gvinaxavs
    ziarebaSi;
    Sinagani cxebiT
    mas metad vimkiT.
  6. jvari aRrmavebs am
    urTierTobas;
    mas metad amaRlebs
    sulis CasunTqva.
  7. is gvaTavisuflebs
    codvili `mesgan~;
    es urTierToba
    RmerTSi migviyvans.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    495. (ing. 738)

  1. yovelgvar sicocxles Tan sdevs,
    garkveuli grZnoba;
    CvenSi myof marad sicocxles,
    aqvs RvTiuri grZnoba.
  2. rac maRalia sicocxle,
    grZnoba aqvs maRali;
    RvTis sicocxle umarles ars
    Tavisi SegrZnebiT.
  3. CvenSia sicocxlis grZnoba,
    es RvTis grZnoba aris;
    es grZnoba cxovrobs Cvens sulSi,
    sikeTes Warbobs is.
  4. Cven SigniT aris es grZnoba,
    Cvens Rrma cnobierSi;
    ganarCevs yovels Signidan,
    asaxavs nebas RvTiss.
  5. RmerTs Cven am grZnobiT SevicnobT,
    sicocxlis am grZnobiT;
    amas ar sWirdeba brZola _
    ars TavisTavadi.
  6. sicocxleSi zrda metad xdis
    am grZnobas gamWriaxs;
    rac metad varT sicocxleSi,
    is metad magrdeba.
  7. sicocxlis grZnobis varjiSiT
    Cvens suls aqvs siqvele;
    RvTis am Sinagani grZnobiT,
    ziareba gvaqvs Cven.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    496. (ing. 739)

  1. uflisgan xelaxlaSobilebs aqvT
    Sinagani mdidari Secnoba;
    garegnuli swavlebebis nacvlad
    gvWirdeba, SevicnoT RmerTi srulad.
  2. umaRles saukuno sicocxles
    aqvs RvTaebrivi sruli unari,
    rom misiT gvqondes Cven RvTis Secnoba,
    da ara swavleba garegnuli.
  3. Cvens gonebSi da Cvens gulzea
    sicocxlis kanoni Cadebuli;
    is gvmarTavs, rom RmerTi SevimecnoT
    da ara swavleba garegnuli.
  4. wmida cxeba mkvidrobs Cvens sulSi dRes,
    Cvens gonebas da guls ucxadebs RmerTs;
    am cxebulebiT Cven SevicnobT RmerTs
    metad, vidre es ZaluZs swavlebebs.
  5. CvenSi samerTiani RmerTia
    mkvidri, moqmedi da aqtiuri,
    rom misi am Sinagani grZnobiT
    SevicnoT RmerTi umaRles doniT.
  6. es Secnoba gvacilebs garegnul
    adamianur codnas, laparaks;
    Cven mudam sulSi unda vicxovroT
    da viaroT am grZnobis Tanaxmad.
  7. roca qristeSi, RvTis sicocxleSi
    vcxovrobT, viqceviT Sinagan grZnobiT,
    metad gveqneba SigniT es grZnoba,
    RmerTic Canergavs Tavis Zes CvenSi.
  8. swored am cocxali SegrZnebiT gvaqvs
    RmerTTan ziareba sicocxleSi;
    RmerTi Tavis sisavses gvimJRavnebs
    swored am dafaruli SecnobiT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    497. (ing. 740)

  1. gankacebis principi aris
    RmerTisa da kacis Serwyma;
    urTierTmoqmedeba maTi
    RmerTis gegmis Sesrulebad.
  2. RmerTs hyavs adamiani, raTa
    gamoxatuleba hqondes;
    kaci xom RmerTis qonebaa
    ase gamoxatavs is RmerTs.
  3. RvTis sibrZnis saCveneblad kacSi
    man gamosyidva Canerga;
    mTel qmnilebas adamianiT
    gadarCena euwyeba.
  4. RmerTis msaxureba Cvens droSi _
    misi da kacis Sromaa;
    RmerTi kacTan mWidro kavSirSi
    Sromobs ase ganuwyvetlad.
  5. RmerTi martodmarto ar Sromobs,
    arc kaci msaxurobs martod,
    RmerTi da kaci erTad Sromobs,
    rom RmerTis gegmam ididos.
  6. gankacebis principi yvelas
    gvWirdeba msaxurebaSi,
    niWebSi Tu moqmedebisas,
    rom vmsaxurebdeT viT erTi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    498. (ing. 741)

  1. RmerTma Zeebad gangvsazRvra,
    uwinares qmnilebis,
    rom suliT CvenTvis moeca
    saxeba Tavisi Zis,
    rom pirmSo gamxdariyo Ze,
    uwin mxolodSobili,
    rom erTad mas da missav Zmebs
    gamoexataT RmerTi.
  2. RvTaebriv xelaxlaSobiT
    RmerTis Zeebi gavxdiT,
    Tumc miRebad pirmSoobis,
    zrda gvmarTebs simwifeSi.
    simwifis asaks mivaRwevT,
    RvTis Zis adgils miviRebT;
    RvTis Zeobas gavacxadebT,
    srulqmnil zomas miviRebT.
  3. suli, mSvinva da sxeuli,
    unda emsgavsos qristes;
    es moxdeba sisruleSi
    roca mova uflis dRe.
    srul Zeobas vpovebT Cveni
    sxeulis gamosyidviT;
    saboloo gardasaxviT,
    aRsruldeba neba RvTis.
  4. saboloo gardasaxva
    gagvawmidanebs srulad;
    didebaSi gadagviyvans
    Cven RmerTi Tavis ZesTan.
    mTeli qmnileba moelis
    RvTis ZeTa gamoCenas,
    rom Jamma Tavisuflebis
    Caanacvlos monoba.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    499. (ing. 742)

  1. adamiani Sedgeba
    suliT, mSvinviT da sxeuliT,
    rom RvTis gegma aRasrulos
    da rom daimkvidros man is.
  2. sxeuli gare mxarea,
    rom Cven aRviqvaT samyaro;
    rom SevexoT gare sagnebs,
    da rom Tavi gamovxatoT.
  3. mSvinva Sida nawilia _
    is `mea~ adamianis;
    misi wyalobiT exeba
    fsikikur samyaros kaci.
  4. suli ki yvelaze Rrmaa,
    misiT Cven ufals vRebulobT;
    suli RvTis SegrZnebas gvaZlevs,
    vxedavT sulier samyaros.
  5. mSvinvas sami nawili aqvs _
    goneba, grZnobebi, neba;
    maTi wyalobiT Cven vavlenT
    adamianur bunebas.
  6. sulsac sami nawili aqvs:
    sindisi, urTierToba,
    intuicia _ rom kacma
    RmerTs uZRvnas Tayvaniscema.
  7. mSvinviT unda avirCioT
    RmerTi, rom mas daveufloT,
    suliT is unda miviRoT,
    sxeuliT ki gamovxatoT.
  8. suls sWirdeba axlad Soba,
    RmerTis sicocxlis miReba;
    mSvinvas _ RvTisgan gardasaxva,
    sxeuls _ qristes msgavsad yofna.
  9. am sam etapze muSaobs
    ufali adamianSi,
    rom ase Seerwyas is kacs _
    misiT gamoxatos Tavi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    500. (ing. 743)

  1. RmerTma Cven Segvqmna WurWlebad
    rom gamogvexata is;
    guliT _ rom is gvyvareboda;
    suliT _ rom miviRoT is.
  2. guliT is unda miviRoT,
    suliT _ mas daveufloT;
    mas vRebulobT viT sicocxles,
    rom Cven is gamovxatoT.
  3. satanam guli gagvixrwna,
    man Cveni suli mokla,
    rom ufals ar SevxebodiT _
    Cveni meTi gvecxovra.
  4. guli da suli ufalma
    gagviaxla, dagvixsna,
    rom SevZloT misi miReba
    da misi Seyvareba.
  5. Cveni gulis ganaxlebiT
    RmerTs mivsdevT siyvarulSi,
    xolo sulis siaxleSi
    mas Cven axlad vexebiT.
  6. uflisadmi Cveni guli
    iyos sufTa da wminda,
    sulSi ki viyoT Raribni,
    RvTisken viswrafvoT mudam.
  7. ufalo, guls siyvaruli _
    suls Zala ar mogvaklo,
    rom Cven sulis siaxleSi
    gamudmebiT SegexoT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    501. (ing. 744)

  1. saTanado guli gvmarTebs
    uflis winaSe Cven,
    rom mis simdidres mis madlSi
    srulad vRebulobdeT.
  2. Cven gvWirdeba sufTa guli,
    goneba _ naTeli,
    rom mis gonebasa da guls
    CavwvdeT sinaTleSi.
  3. Cven gvWirdeba siyvaruliT
    anTebuli guli,
    grZnobebi _ moSurneobiT
    anTebuli misTvis.
  4. Cven unda viyoT morCili
    guliTa da nebiT,
    damyoli, Tumc mtkice nebiT,
    RmerTis nebisaTvis.
  5. guli msjavrs ar unda gvdebdes
    Cven winaSe RmerTis;
    gvWirdeba sufTa sindisi,
    sisxliT ganbanili.
  6. ufalo, mogveci guli
    Senze motmasnuli,
    rom Sen geziaroT, viyoT
    Cven sisavse Seni.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    502. (ing. 745)

  1. suli xar ufalo, axla,
    Cvens sulSi mcxovrebi;
    ori suli erTi gaxda,
    erTobis momcemi.
  2. Seni suli Cems sulTan dRes,
    atarebs mowmobas,
    rom RmerTi mamis Svilebi
    da memkvidreni varT.
  3. Cveni suliT Sen gexebiT
    da simdidriT vtkbebiT;
    minarevebis gareSe
    Sens Tavs gvaZlev suliT.
  4. dae, viaroT Cven suliT,
    gamogyveT yovelTvis;
    Seni suli win wargviZRves,
    agvavsos sinaTliT.
  5. sulSi, sulis meSveobiT
    vcxovrobT da Tayvans gcemT;
    Cvens sulSi xar da am suliT
    mudam gvaZliereb.
  6. Cven aRvavlenT locvebs Sen win,
    sulSi sulTan erTad.
    Sen oxrav gamouTqmelad,
    viT suli CvenSi xar.
  7. Cveni sulisken vbrundebiT,
    aq gekontaqtebiT;
    aq, am sulSi viziarebT,
    qonebas RvTaebrivs.
  8. ra erToba warmoiSva
    ori sulis SerwyiT!
    Seni suli cxovrobs CvenSi,
    Cveni suli SenSi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    503. (ing. 746)

  1. ufalo, sulisgan samSvinvlis
    garCeva gvaswavle Cven,
    rom SegicnoT Sen rogorc suli,
    da Cvens sulSi SegerwyaT Sen.
  2. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, rom mSvinva uarvyoT,
    rom gamogyveT Sen Cvens sulSi da
    viT suli gamogiyenoT.
  3. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, xorcze ar movmarToT
    goneba, raTa `mem~ da codvam
    Cven aRarasdros SegvboWos.
  4. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, rom mSvinvierni ar
    viyoT, rogorc sulierebma
    SevZloT yvelafris garCeva.
  5. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, Cveni `me~ amxile,
    rom viyenebdeT masze Cven jvars
    da mxolod SeniT vcxovrobdeT.
  6. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, mSvinva gardasaxe,
    dagvamsgavse Cven Sens saxebas,
    sanam mizans mivaRwevdeT.
  7. ufalo, gvaswavle garCeva
    sulis, mogvec sityva Seni,
    rom gaiyos suli da mSvinva,
    vcxovrobdeT yovlad wmidaSi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    504. (ing. 747)

  1. RmerTis taZris yovlad wminda
    aris wyalobis adgili;
    iq Zevs RmerTis kidobani,
    iq ufals xvdebian mRvdlebi.
  2. axla Cven varT RvTis taZari;
    Cvens siRrmeSi Cven gvaqvs suli;
    masSi RmerTi da qristea
    damkvidrebuli viT suli.
  3. am adgilas yvelaferi
    RmerTi qristeSia CvenTvis;
    swored aq xdis wmida suli
    sinamdviled ufals CvenTvis.
  4. swored am sulis nawilSi
    Cven vmkvidrobT qristesTan erTad;
    swored suliT vurTierTobT
    RmerTTan da iq vcemT mas Tayvans.
  5. sulSi aris qriste miwa,
    sadac vcxovrobT, vtkbebiT uxvad;
    swored masSi vebrZviT mtrebsac,
    da vflobT qristes xelmwifebas.
  6. Cven unda SevicnoT suli,
    gavarCioT is mSvinvisgan,
    vicxovroT yovlad wmindaSi
    da mivRwioT mis mizans.
  7. mSvinva unda mivatovoT,
    RvTis dasveneba rom vpovoT,
    qristes srulad daveufloT,
    RmerTis gegma SevasruloT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    505. (ing. 748)

  1. jvriT amoicaniT suli,
    mSvinva sul moakvdineT;
    jvari zideT, `me~ uaryveT,
    mudam sulSi iareT.
  2. jvriT amoicaniT suli,
    RmerTis cocxali sityviT,
    suli mSvinvisgan gamijneT,
    rom iaroT swori gziT.
  3. jvriT amoicaniT suli,
    gonebis siaxleSi,
    grZnobebi gqondeT miZRvnili,
    neba gqondeT morCili.
  4. jvriT amoicaniT suli;
    ganvleT farda glejili,,
    xorcic, mSvinvac Seimusra,
    suli aris wamyvani.
  5. jvriT amoicaniT suli,
    aq, wmidaTa wmidaSi

    mis:
    simSvideSi gelodebi,
    msurs Seni neba Sevicno;
    gamaciskrovne, vxedavde,
    wmida sulo!

  2. Cems yurebs esmodes Seni
    WeSmaritebis xma naTlad;
    yvela siyalbe gaqres Cemgan
    am tkbili xmis mosmenisas.
  3. Cems bages Seexe, raTa
    wyalobaze daamowmos.
    amavse siyvaruliT, raTa
    Sens SvilebTan veziaro.
  4. goneba gamixsen, SevZlo,
    Sens siyvaruls Cavwvde metad;
    Sen CemTan xar, ris meSinia?
    mxolod sinaTle msurs Sengan.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    545. (ing. 811)

  1. SewevnisaTvis SenTan movdivar,
    mSieri guliT, mwyurvale suliT;
    Sen xar erTaderTi, vinc mWirdeba,
    rom gamiqres SimSili, wyurvili.

    mis:
    mkvebe, ufalo, damarwyule;
    gamiqre SimSili, wyurvili;
    mavseb tkbobiT,sicocxlis Zala xar;
    gamiqre SimSili, wyurvili.

  2. sicocxlis wyali da sakvebi xar;
    gamomacocxleb, suls gamimxneveb;
    Zlier msurs SevWamo, Sevsva Sengan;
    kiTxviT, locviT SeniT uxvad davtkbe.
  3. sityva xar, visSic RvTis sisavsea,
    xar suli, vinc Cems sicocxled RmerTs xdis;
    sityvaSi vtkbebi, rogorc sakvebiT,
    Sen rogorc suli xar wyali CemTvis.
  4. zecidan mosuli sakvebi xar,
    CemTvis gaipe, rom Sengan Sevsva;
    auracxeli momarageba,
    Sewevna Sengan moedineba.
  5. sityvaSi xar suli da sicocxle;
    me SeniT uxvad rom vnadimobde;
    Sen rogorc suli, Cems sulSi mkvidrob,
    raTa am sulidan mudam vsvamde.
  6. axla, Sens sityvasTan mosvliT vtkbebi,
    gWam sanam ar gaqreba SimSili;
    axla, Cems sulSi Senken vbrundebi,
    gsvam, sanam ar gaqreba wyurvili.
  7. Sengan SevWam da Sevsvam, ufalo,
    vikvebebi kiTxviT da vsvam locviT;
    kiTxviT da locviT, SegWam da daglev,
    locva-kiTxviT xdebi Cemi wili.
  8. o, Cemi nadimi xar, ufalo,
    mavseb Seni suliTa da sityviT;
    dae, ufalo iyavi marad
    nadimi, romelic arsad Tqmula.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    546. (ing. 812)

  1. movdivar, ufalo,
    Cems guls Sen swyurixar.
    damapure da Semasvi,
    damatkbe sruliad.
  2. umziros Sens saxes,
    amas natrobs guli.
    o, rogor Zlier swyurixar,

  3. guli xarobs Seni

    guli savse aris.
  5. msurs rom SenTan davrCe
    metad mogipovo,
    cocxali sityviT da locviT,
    rom gadmoiRvaro.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    547. (ing. 813)

  1. madlis taxtis winaSe var,

  2. Sens brwyinvale saxes vucqer,

  11. o, msurs es urTierToba _
    kiTxva, locva, SenTan Serwyma;

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    548. (ing. 814)

  1. puriT ki ar cocxlobs kaci,
    aramed RmerTis bagidan
    gamosuli yvela sityviT.
    gvaqvs sicocxle maTi WamiT.
  2. Cven varT Seqmnilebi da gvaqvs:
    sxeuli, mSvinva da suli.
    Rrma nawili _ suli gvaqvs, rom

  3. fizikuri sicocxlisTvis

  4. Sen xar suli, Seni sityviT,

  5. Seni sityvis misaRebad,

  6. Seni sityva unda vWamoT

  7. codna mxolod gonebaSi,

  8. yvelaze siRrmiseulad,

  9. sulis varjiSi gvaswavle,
    sityvis kiTxvisas, ufalo,

    SeniT momaragebuli.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    549. (ing. 815)

  1. qriste sityva da sulia,
    da rogorc suli sityvaSi;

    dae, suli Sens sityvaSi,
    gTxov, gamoixatos Cemgan.

    550. (ing. 816)

  1. RvTis sityvas sicocxled viRebT

    mTeli misi sisavsiT.
    rom arc erTi gagvitacos
    qarma ucxo swavlebis.
  7. sxeuls, raTa aaSenos,
    RmerTma misca niWebi.
    wmidanebis srulyofisTvis
    maTsav msaxurebaSi.
    gavixadoT Zveli kaci!
    axali SevimosoT!
    ganvvaxldeT goneba-sulSi,
    qriste gamovavlinoT.
  8. udidesi saidumlo!
    qriste da eklesia!
    viT kaci sxeulze _ qristec
    zrunavs eklesiaze.
    siyvarulSi Seewira
    eklesiisaTvis, rom
    is gaewmidanebina,
    gaexada umanko.
  9. eklesiaa: sxeuli,
    erTi axali kaci,
    patarZali, Semosili
    RmerTis sruli saWurvliT,
    jari, romelic ibrZvis, rom
    bolo mouRos RvTis mters.
    dgas medgrad, agrZelebs brZolas,
    yvela am locviT is dRes.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    560. (ing. 824)

  1. eklesia _ sxeuli,
    mamis samkvidroa;
    moxmobilTa krebuli,
    RmerTis Serwyma kacTan;
    arCeuli Seqmnamde,
    jvriT gamosyiduli;
    misi buneba, dgoma,
    aris zeciuri.
  2. is axal qmnilebaSi
    dabada ufalma;
    RmerT sulSi moinaTla,
    sityviT gawmidanda;
    qriste misi Tavia,
    SigTavsi, sicocxle;
    masTan amaRlebaSi,
    mtrebs Telavs fexTa qveS.
  3. qristea eklesiis
    myari saZirkveli;
    qristesebr is yovelmxriv
    aris RvTaebrivi;
    misi asoni suliT
    jvarcmulni arian;
    aRdgomaSi ki Zvirfas
    qvebad Sendebian.
  4. misi elementia
    erTi: RmerTi, suli,
    ufali; da naTloba,
    rwmena da sxeuli;
    samerTiani RmerTi
    aris mis wevrebSi,
    romelnic erTdebian
    didebis imedSi.
  5. asoebi arian
    yoveli eridan;
    klasebis ganurCevlad
    gaxdnen erTi srulad;
    masSi ar aqvs adgili
    iudevels, berZens;
    rogorc axali kaci:
    yvelaSia qriste.
  6. sxeuli aris erTi _
    samyaroseuli;
    TiTo qalaqSi erTi
    eklesia aris;
    mmarTveloba maT yvelas
    aqvT adgilobrivi;
    moziareoba ki _
    samyaroseuli.
  7. axal ierusalims
    aqvs gamovlineba _
    adgilobriv krebebze
    misi niSnebi Cans.
    RmerTi qristeSi rogroc
    lamparSi anaTebs;
    yvela sasanTle RmerTis
    saxebas atarebs.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    561. (ing. 829)

  1. eklesiis Tesli TviT qristea,
    daTesili Cvens gulSi sicocxled;
    izrdeba viT xorbali, fqvils gvaZlevs,
    rom purma RmerTs da kacs tkboba misces.
  2. satanam cru morwmuneebi viT
    RvarZli Seuria xorbals Soris;
    dabneulobis mosatanad, rom
    maT ver Seasrulon gegma RmerTis.
  3. eklesiis sicocxle, viT mdogvi
    mcenares hgavs, qristesgan izrdeba;
    dafaruli, Zlier pataraa,
    Tumca kargia gamosakvebad.
  4. satanam Secvala am mcenaris
    buneba da garegnuli forma;
    uzarmazar xed gazarda, sadac
    borotebma Tavi moiyara.
  5. satanam dacemul `eklesias~
    warmarTuli Cveulebac misca;
    xorblis comSi safuari Serwya,
    misi siwminde mTlianad gaxrwna.
  6. magram qriste, viT sicocxle Tavis
    wmidebs gardasaxavs Zvirfas qvebad;
    Tavis eklesiis, samefosTvis
    maT gaxdis Zvirfas saSen masalad.
  7. eklesia izrdeba qristeSi
    gardaisaxeba da Sendeba;
    is Zvirfasi margaliti aris
    mindorSi dafaruli ganZia.
  8. ufalo, gamogvyavi `RvarZlisgan~
    gvixseni, ar viyoT `xis~ nawili;
    yovelgvar safuars mogvaSore,
    viyoT sakvebi SenTvis, sxvebisTvis.
  9. yoveldRiurad gagvzarde RmerTSi,
    gardavisaxoT, SenSi avSendeT;
    Sens sxeulad, raTa gamogxatoT,
    da CvenSi Sens samefos xedavde.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    562. (ing. 1274)

  1. Svid adgilobriv sasanTles,
    vxedavT gamocxadebaSi;
    naTeli gakveTilia
    aq uflis aRdgenisaTvis.
  2. maTTvis naTqvami sityvebi,
    CvenTvisac aris aseve;
    miviRoT gafrTxileba, rom
    uflis mizani Sesruldes.
  3. naTeli sityva efesos:
    `pirvel siyvaruls nu toveb;
    mxolod saqmes nu akeTeb;
    moinanie uflisken!~
  4. yvela uflisken mivbrundeT,
    sxva siyvaruli codvaa;
    mis daZaxils movusminoT _
    es yvelaze mTavaria.
  5. smirnas, tanjul eklesias:
    `gansacdelebs gauZeli,
    erTgul iyav sikvdilamde~
    (sxeuliT da samSvinveliT).
  6. nu uaryof tanjvebs Sensas,
    unda mokvdes bunebrivi;
    ufali gcdis daumtkico
    mas pirveli siyvaruli.
  7. pergamo: qristianobis
    wuTisofelze qorwils xsnis;
    erTgul antipas aq vxedavT,
    vinc yvelafers aRudga win.
  8. gveSinodes, ar SevideT,
    sofelTan qorwinebaSi;
    uflis sityvas movusminoT,
    viyoT gamoyofilebi.
  9. Tiatira Seezava
    mTeli ZaliT wuTisofels;
    fqvilSi safuari Cado,
    da meZavi mxecs atarebs.
  10. ufalo, amxile srulad
    CvenSi Sezaveba msgavsi;
    Cven uarvyofT rac Sen ar xar
    gagvxade SenTvis miZRvnilni.
  11. sardis magaliTze mosCans:
    sicocxle _ erTaderTi gza!
    Tavs cocxlad Tvlis, Tumc mkvdaria,
    uflis Sexeba sWirdeba.
  12. ufalo, gvsurs sicocxlis gziT,
    sikvdilze rom gavimarjvoT;
    sikvdils gaveqceT da mxolod
    sicocxliT savseni viyoT.
  13. axla ki filadelfia,
    rac aqvs Zlier CaeWidos:
    Zmur siyvaruls, saxels, sityvas;
    amiT ufals Zlier atkbobs.
  14. rogorc Zmebi, Cven erTi varT;
    erTi sicocxle mogveca;
    Tu sityvas, saxels davicavT,
    vxdebiT RmerTis nageboba.
  15. daodikiaSi vxedavT:
    maT vinc ambobs: `mdidari var~.
    ganudga filadelfias
    ufali gareT dgas karTan.
  16. nelTbiloba moviSoroT,
    mudmivad viwvodeT sulSi;
    sicocxlis gancda miviRoT,
    masTan erTad mefobisTvis.
  17. ufalo, dagvanaTe dRes,
    mxolod Sens gzas gvsurs gamovyveT;
    scxe Cvens Tvalebs, xedva mogvec,
    o, aRdgena moipove.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    563. (ing. 831)

  1. eklesiaa wmidanTa
    erTobaSi cxovreba;
    maradiuli erToba
    maTSi mcxovreb suls moaqvs.
    amitom ewodeba mas
    sulis erTianoba;
    es erToba efuZneba
    rwmenis memkvidreobas.
  2. wmidanTa Zvirfasi rwmena
    moicavs qristes da mis
    gamomsyidvel samuSaos _
    wmidaa, erTaderTi.
    yvela wmida erTi aris,
    TanxmobaSi modian;
    am saerTo rwmenis qoniT
    arsebobs eklesia.
  3. eklesia qristesia,
    samyaroSi erTia;

    zustad misi msgavsia.
    maTi elementebia:
    RmerTi, ufali, suli,

  4. eklesia dgas erTobis

    sulis moTxovnaa es.

    sasicocxlo kavSirebs;
    urTierToba aSenebs,

    Seni gulis Rrma survili,
    sul mTlianad Sesruldes;
    RvTis maradiuli gegma
    srulad ganxorcieldes.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    564. (ing. 832)

  1. RmerTis Ze qriste, misi gamosyidva,

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    565. (ing. 834)

  1. ufalo, qvakuTxedi xar,
    RvTis mier aRdgomaSi;
    iudevlebma uargyves,
    Zvirfasi xar RvTis TvalSi.
    SeniT gvaqvs gadarCena da
    SenTan vSendebiT axla;
    iudeveli, warmarTi _
    cxovrobs erT axal kacad.
  2. gapobili klde xar, raTa
    mokla kacis wyurvili;
    Sen dageyrdnos myife xalxi
    aaSenon RvTis saxli.
    nacado da saimedo,
    saZirkvlis qvav sionze;
    eklesiis sayrdeni xar,
    mas uyri safuZvels Sen.
  3. jojoxeTis bWeni cdilobs
    eklesiis daZlevas;
    Tumc is dgas uryevad, mtkiced
    radgan Senze Sendeba.
    Sens Zalauflebas is flobs,
    xsnis da kravs kidec SenSi;
    mtris tyveebs aTavisuflebs,
    mohyavs Sens samefoSi.
  4. sicocxlis cocxali qva xar,
    Zvirfasi da rCeuli;
    Cvenc cocxal qvebad gagvxade,
    SenTan varT srulad erTi.
    vSendebiT erTobliv taZrad,
    rom aq RmerTma icxovros;
    wmida samRvdeloeba varT,
    rom mas msxverpli SevwiroT.
  5. ufalo, daviTis Ze xar,
    RmerTis taZars aSeneb;
    mefe da mRvdelmTavari xar,
    gegmis Sesasruleblad.
    RmerTisTvis marTav _ viT mefe,
    yvelas mas umorCileb;
    RvTis TandaswrebaSi _ viT mRvdels,
    maT uZRvi mis winaSe.
  6. taxtidan Zalauflebas
    moaqvs CvenTvis mSvidoba;
    mdinares _ urTierToba,
    uxvi momarageba.
    am yvelafris erTad gancdiT,
    sruldeba RmerTis gegma;
    Sen rogorc mefe da mRvdeli,
    aSeneb RmerTis saxls kvlav.
  7. RmerTi xar, vinc xorci gaxda,
    RmerTi, kaci SenSia;
    RvTis didebis taZari xar,
    da avlen mis didebas.
    RmerTis da adamianis
    Serwymaa eklesia;
    yvela wevri am sxeulis
    RmerTis gegmisTvisaa.
  8. maradiulo samkvidro,
    Cveno sacxovrebelo;
    vtkbebiT, radgan aq Sen gvicav,
    Cven mxolod SenSi vcovrobT.
    Cveni sawmidari Sen xar,
    aq vmkvidrobT RmerTTan erTad;
    RmerTis Tandaswreba gvaqvs da
    Tayvans vcemT mas uwyvetad.
  9. qvakuTxedi, saZirkveli,
    Tavkiduri, klde da qva;
    eklesia, sawmidari,
    mSenebelic Sena xar.
    gaqebT yvelafrisTvis vinc xar!
    mSveniero ufalo!
    Cvenc rogorc cocxalma qvebma,
    Seni saxli vaSenoT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    566. (ing. 837)

  1. gaqebT, ufalo gegmisTvis _

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    567. (ing. 838)

  1. Sens gegmas vafaseb Zlier
    masSi vxedav Sens savanes;

    Seni dideba gamoCndes.
  2. savanis centrSi isvenebs

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    569. (ing. 840)

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    570. (ing. 841)

  1. o, Cemi sicocxle

    572. (ing. 843)

  1. o, STambere sicocxlis suTqva,

    uflis gamoCenis grgvinvaa es Tu
    misi xalxis locvis musikaa?
  2. is namdvilad modis da aTasi xma
    SesZaxebs wmindanebs da yru-munjebs,
    namdvilad mova, is vinc daifica
    `me moval!~ da miwa gaixarebs
  3. daifica, rogor ar gavaRmerToT?
    nuTu kvlav varT sasowarkveTilni?
    modiT, Cveni Tavi mas CavabaroT,
    mis fexebTan davdoT Cveni tvirTi
  4. sicocxliT iqneba es Tu sikvdiliT,
    is sakmarisi iqneba CemTvis,
    qristea dasawyisic, dasasrulic,
    qriste Cemi sawyisi, sasruli.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    701. (ing. 970)

  1. didebul gamocxadebas
    RvTis Zeebisas elis
    mTeli qmnileba, rom iyos
    monobisgan daxsnili
  2. amaoebas hmorCilebs,
    kvnesis mTeli qmnileba
    da xrwnilebis monobisgan
    moelis srulad daxsnas
  3. aseve Cvenc voxravT, sanam
    mivaRwevT srul simwifes,
    moveliT Svilobas srulad
    davemsgavsebiT qristes
  4. amisaTvis TviT suli oxravs,
    surs qristes dagvamsgavsos
    erTad muSaobs yoveli,
    rom suliT gardagvsaxos.
  5. RmerTs mivyavarT didebaSi,
    erT dResac gangvadidebs
    mTlianad gagvJRenTs misi ZiT,
    srulad gagvawmidanebs
  6. didebis TavisuflebiT
    daixsneba qmnileba,
    saqoneli daTvTan moZovs,
    bavSvi dawveba vefxvTan
  7. qristes Tanamemkvidreni
    daveuflebiT Cven ganZs,
    Cvens ufal, qristesTan erTad
    RvTis didebas movitanT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    702. (ing. 1321)

  1. madli naboZebi RvTisgan
    srulad aris RvTis Ze,

    misia siuxve.
    aRemateba gagebas,
    gasaocaria
    erT dros sasowarkveTilni

  2. monobis mZime uRlis qveS
    wevs mTeli qmnileba
    RvTis ZeTa gamocxadebiT
    is daxsnil iqneba.
    maradiuli ganzraxva

  3. mirtis xeebad iqceva,

  4. RvTis madlis Rrma samuSao

  5. angelozni RvTis winaSe

    uerTdebian RvTis,
    yvelafrisTvis,rac dagegma,
    mteri ganaqarva,

  6. ase rom, siamovnebiT

    yovel dRe darigdes,
    xSirad farulia, mcire
    madls, romelsac viRebT,
    RmerTi inergeba CvenSi
    da brwyinavs dRiTi dRe.

    704. (ing. 1303)

  1. RvTis samefo axlovdeba:

    centridan napirebisken,
    yvelaferi gaJRinTos,
    ganaaxlos samSvinveli,
    Cvens gulSi daivanos.
  5. vSendebiT ra sicocxleSi,
    vmagrdebiT siyvarulSi,
    aRasrulebs diad gegmas,
    arsebuls, Tavis gulSi.
    o ufalo, did WurWelSi,
    erTSi, SeniT savseSi,
    rom SevZloT Cven CaSeneba,
    gaizarde Sen CvenSi.
  6. eklesia didebaSi _
    jami! da Sesruleba!
    es erToblivi WurWeli
    daitevs mis didebas,
    raTa aRsruldes dRes misi
    Canafiqri maradi,
    Cven varT Seni miznisaTvis,
    erTi axali kaci!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    718. (ing. 972)

  1. RmerTis fiqri isaa,
    rom iyos erTi kacTan,
    iyos misTvis yoveli,
    rom Sesruldes RvTis gegma.
  2. kaci _ Tixis WurWeli,
    suliT, mSvinviT sxeuliT _
    Seiqmna, rom mieRo
    Tavis sicocxled RmerTi.
  3. RvTis sicocxlis dinebiT,
    kaci Zvirfas qvad xdeba,
    RvTis savaned iqceva,
    rom aCvenos dideba.
  4. es qalaqi aSenda
    RmerTiT, misi moTxovniT,
    mis guls atkbobs axali
    es ierusalimi.
  5. es saxlia wmidebis,
    Serwyma RmerTis da kacis _
    nafiqri mamis nebiT,
    Seqmnamde wuTisoflis.
  6. mis centrSi aris taxti
    RmerTisa da qristesi;
    iqidan mdinared Cqefs
    rogorc sicocxle suli.
  7. qriste sicocxlis xea
    nakadis dinebaSi,
    RvTis nayofi moaqvs viT
    umaRlesi sakvebi.
  8. RmerTi qristeSi lamprad
    anaTebs mTel qalaqSi,
    fantavs sikvdilis ukuns
    RvTaebrivi sinaTliT.
  9. aw RmerTi aris kacSi,
    kaci ki aris RmerTSi;
    kaci RmerTs gamoxatavs
    da is savsea RmerTiT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    719. (ing. 974)

  1. is eZebda qalaqs, iyo karavSi,
    iyo xizani, didebis lodinSi;
    misi nugeSi iyo RmerTis aRTqma,
    is ar eZebda miwier didebas.

    mis:
    diad ars qalaqi!
    aq RmerTi kacTan saukunod cxovrobs.

  2. is eZebda qalaqs, RvTis momzadebuls;
    miwis sasaxleSi yofna as ar surs,
    is uyurebda samefo samyofels,
    romelsac RmerTi dahpirda Tvis xiznebs.
  3. is eZebda qalaqs, ukuagdebda
    miwis didebas, oxravda xSirad gzas,
    magram qalaqis fiqriT kvlav mReroda,
    uxeSi gza mokled eCveneboda.
  4. is eZebda qalaqs, da Cvenc massaviT varT;
    ufalo, gvwams, Sen amzadeb am qalaqs,
    rogorc maradiul xvedrs imaTTvis, vinc
    xiznad cxovrobs iesosTan karavSi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    720.

  1. roca gavivli sarbiels
    da vpoveb gamarjvebas,
    uflis didebaSi amitaceben;
    Tu rwmenas SevinarCuneb
    bolomde, wmida qalaqs
    vici, jildod miviReb.

    mis:
    didebul wmida qalaqSi
    male amitaceben _
    wmida axal ierusalimSi!
    gamarjvebulebTan erTad
    mosCqefs qebis nakadi _
    axal wmida qalaqSi!

  2. miwaze viT mwiri vdivar
    vxarob, Tumc var tanjuli,
    ukeTes miwaze moveli Sesvlas;
    Tumca sxvebs surT miwieri
    simdidreTa moxveWa,
    me wmida qalaqs veli.
  3. Tumc gadameRala ferxni
    rTul gzaze siaruliT,
    im qalaqis gaxsenebiT vmxnevdebi;
    Tumc TvalT cremli xSirad momdis,
    jildosken Cemi guli _
    qalaqisken iswrafis.
  4. mtkiced viswrafvi miznisken,
    SeuCereblad vibrZvi,
    rom vinZlo movipove RmerTis jildo;
    viviwyeb rac warsulSia
    da gavrbivar miznisken,
    wmida qalaqisaken.

    mis:
    wmida qalaqSi vicxovreb
    RvTis madlSi, siyvarulSi _
    wmida axal ierusalimSi!
    aq xarobs yvela wmidani
    dideba ismis uflis _
    axal wmida qalaqSi!



    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    721. (ing. 975)

  1. dasawyisSi iyo mxolod baRi,
    bolos ki _ kvadratuli qalaqi;
    am baRSi iyo qmnilebis centri,
    RvTis Senoba mTavrdeba qalaqiT.
  2. qalaqSic da baRSic _ orivegan
    moCans mdinare da xe sicocxlis,
    maTSi vxedavT qristes viT Sewevnas
    da suls, rogorc dinebas sicocxlis.
  3. qalaqSic da baRSic _ orivegan
    Cans sami Zvirfasi substancia _
    oqros, margalits, Zvirfas qvebs vxedavT,
    RvTis SenobisTvis bevri ram Cans aq.
  4. Tumc baRSi es sami Zvirfasi ram
    viT masala Zevs mxolod miwaSi,
    diad qalaqSi ki yvelaferi
    aris erTurTSi aSenebuli.
  5. baRSi kaci Tixisgan Seiqmna,
    ase qmna ufalma is bunebiT;
    sicocxlis xes iyo kacis miRma,
    jer ar iyo sicocxled mis SigniT.
  6. qalaqSi ki didebuli xea,
    erTobliv `kacSi~ is izrdeba da
    avlens TviT qristes rogorc sicocxles,
    rogorc kacis Sinagan Sewevnas.
  7. swored qalaqisTvis iyo kaci
    axlad Sobili, gardasaxuli
    wminda oqrod, margalitad, qvebad,
    qristes sxeulad, masze namsgavsi.
  8. baRis Signic iyo patarZali,
    da is iyo damxmare adamis;
    qalaqSidac moCans patarZali,
    qristes sisavse da sixaruli.
  9. qalaqi RvTis Sromis gvirgvinia,
    erToblioba gamarTlebulnis;
    aw masSi RmerTs aqvs samkvidrebeli,
    is qristes Zvirfasi sasZlo aris.
  10. is RmerTs sisruleSi gamoxatavs,
    erToblivad, samyaroseulad;
    qristes diadi sasZlo is aris,
    RmerTis didebas is avlens srulad.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    722. (ing. 976)

  1. ufalo, gamosyidulni
    arian sasZlo Seni,
    Seni sisavse _ sxeuli,
    srulad diddebi masSi.
    masSi Sen xar yvelaferi,
    Sens simdidres avlens is;
    Sens didebas unawileb,
    da Sen mas mTlianad JRenT.

    mis:
    he, wmida qalaqi,
    savse RvTis didebiT!
    RmerTia gamoxatuli
    adamianSi!

  2. Sezavdnen RmerTi da kaci _
    RvTismosaoba didi.
    didebiT damkvidrda RmerTi
    kacSi _ samkvidrebelSi.
    es didebuli WurWeli,
    avlens sisavses RmerTis;
    silamaze moCans masSi
    da siwmide Cveni RvTis.
  3. cocxali Semadgenloba
    gardasaxul wmidebis;
    misi saxebis msgavsebi,
    qvebi _ margalitebi:
    centridan taxtisa RmerTis
    modis cocxali wyali;
    qriste yvavis viT sicocxlis
    xe da moaqvs nayofi.
  4. maradi oqros sasanTle,
    ikavebs qristes naTels;
    RmerTi qristeSi didebiT
    rogorc suli anaTebs!
    gamoxatuleba sruli _
    RmerT-kaci erTmaneTSi;
    urTierTsavane maTi _
    saukuno gegma RvTis.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    723. (ing. 978)

  1. axal ierusalims
    RmerTis brwyinvalebiT,
    axal ca da miwaze
    vxedavT RvTis didebiT.

    mis:
    mas aqvs RmerTis saxeba,
    mas aqvs RmerTis dideba!
    masSi TviT ufalia,
    RvTis am qalaqSi.

  2. margalitiT Sedgeba
    misi karibWeni,
    quCa wminda oqroa,
    Tormeti safuZvliT.
  3. iq Cqefs brolis mdinare,
    uxvi SewevnebiT,
    sicocxlis xec izrdeba,
    gvakmayofilebs is.
  4. iq RmerTi aris `me var~,
    sinaTlis qalaqSi;
    RmerTi kravSi anaTebs,
    iq ar aris bneli.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    724. (ing. 979)

  1. ra didebulad kaSkaSebs,
    wmida ierusalimi;
    RmerTis da kacis samkvidro,
    qriste-kravis patarZali.
  2. yvela drois wmidanebi,
    RmerTis aRTqmis memkvidreni
    Seadgenen am did qalaqs
    Sendebian savaned RvTis.
  3. qalaqi kvadratulia,
    erTi zomis _ yvela mxare;
    Tanaswori yovelimxriv,
    ardaxrili, swormdgomare.
  4. qalaqis quCa oqroa,
    SuSasaviT gamWvirvale,
    es niSnavs, rom mis bunebas,
    xarisxs adgens RvTis sicocxle.
  5. margalitis karibWeSi
    vxedavT gamosyidvas kacis,
    gardasaxuls margalitad
    da mimavals RvTis sferoSi.
  6. Tormetnair Zvirfasi qvis
    mis kedels aqvs saZirkveli;
    cecxliT da wneviT nawrTobi,
    saukuno aqvs mas fasi.
  7. kedeli aqvs iaspisis,
    RvTis didebas srulad avlens;
    RmerTi Tavad hgavs iaspiss,
    kedlidan Cans RvTis sinaTle.
  8. yvela uwmindurebisgan
    qalaqs kedeli gamohyofs;
    masSi yofna ZaluZs mxolod
    margalits, Zvirfas qvebs, oqros.
  9. RmerT-kravi iq taZaria!
    mis diad saxes vixilavT;
    da Cven mis TandaswrebaSi
    vicxovrebT maradiulad.
  10. qalaqs ar aqvs mze da mTvare,
    iq RvTis dideba anaTebs;
    kravi misi lampadaa,
    da is yovelmxriv kaSkaSebs.
  11. RvTisa da kravis taxtidan
    cocxali nakadi mosCqefs,
    da mis orive napirze
    moCans, yvavis sicocxlis xe.
  12. es niSavs, rom RvTis sicocxle
    ar aris mxolod sakvebi,
    mas sdevs RvTis Zalaufleba
    qalaqis yvela adgilSi.
  13. misi wminda oqros quCa
    RvTis bunebas gzad aCvenebs;
    sicocxlis uxvi nayofiT
    moedineba mdinare.
  14. ricxvi Tormeti aRniSnavs
    saukuno xelmwifebas;
    samjer oTxi ki aRniSnavs
    RmerTis kacTan Sezavebas.
  15. masSi sibnele, sikvdili,
    sevda da tkivili wava,
    Zvels axali Caanacvlebs
    RmerTi kacTan damkvidrdeba.
  16. qalaqs RmerTis aqvs saxeba,
    mmarTvelobs mefis magivrad,
    mis gegmas axorcielebs,
    hgvris mas dakmayofilebas.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    725. (ing. 980)

  1. wmidanebis winasaxes
    mTel wmida werilSi vxedavT:
    sasZlos _ RmerTis gasaxarad,
    Senobas _ mosasveneblad.
  2. eklesiis winasaxed
    Zvel aRTqmaSi naTlad vxedavT:
    saxls _ cxovrebisTvis, marTvisTvis,
    patarZals _ kacis mSvenebas.
  3. RmerTma Zvel droSi uwoda
    Tavis xalxs Tavisi coli;
    maT Soris da maTTan erTad
    iyo RvTis saxli, qalaqi.
  4. RmerTi qristeSi movida
    rogorc sasZlosaTvis qmari;
    mewyvilis mosapoveblad
    mas misca sicocxle Tvisi.
  5. aRdgomaSi qriste agebs
    RvTis taZars viT daviTis Ze,
    rom iq RmerTma moisvenos
    da misi neba aRsruldes.
  6. qristes siamovnebaa
    eklesia rogorc sasZlo;
    RmerTis samkvidrebelia,
    raTa man masSi icxovros.
  7. wmida qalaqi iqneba
    saboloo dasruleba
    saxlis, sasZlos winasaxis _
    diad gegmis aRsruleba.
  8. es sasZlo Sehferis qristes,
    misiT is Tavs gamotaxavs;
    is RmerTis savanecaa,
    rom imefos, hpovos Sveba.
  9. is dasrulebaa Sromis,
    romelic RmerTma kacSi qmna;
    gamosyidulebSi Tavs is
    didebaSi gamoxatavs.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    726. (ing. 981)

  1. RmerTma mouyaros Tavi
    yovelives qristeSi;
    qriste iyos Tavi, centri,
    mis saxlmSeneblobaSi.
  2. qriste Tavi aris centri,
    RmerTi masSi _ sinaTle;
    qriste taxtze, RmerTTan erTad
    mis survils Seasrulebs.
  3. qriste, rogorc TviT sicocxle
    Tavs mouyris yvelafers;
    yvela wmida _ RvTis WurWeli
    mis didebas waradgens.
  4. satanis Sxami Sevida
    kacSi, raTa gaexrwna;
    sibnele moitana, rom
    RvTis gegma CaeSala.
  5. qriste movida, Canerga
    Tavi kacSi sicocxled;
    raTa aRar davemonoT
    sikvdilsa da sibneles.
  6. eklesiis meSveobiT
    Tavs mouyris yvelafers;
    Seanawevrebs dids, mcires,
    Seamtkicebs erTmaneTs.
  7. qristes sruli Tavobis qveS
    harmonia ivanebs;
    eklesia sinaTleSi
    qristes erTobas avlens.
  8. sadac qriste aris Tavi
    TanxmobaSia yvela;
    eklesiis sinaTleSi
    TavisuflebiT tkbeba.
  9. gardaxda bneli, sikvdili,
    maTi xvedri _ gaqroba;
    marwuxisgan daxsnilia
    saukunod qmnileba.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    727. (ing. 984)

  1. cocxali wylis mdinarea
    taxtidan momdinare,
    RvTis Zalauflebas avlens,
    urTierTobas gvaZlevs.

    mis:
    es cocxali wylis mdinare
    gvaZlevs urTierTobas;
    mas Tan sdevs Zalaufleba
    yvelgan, sadac is wava.

  2. suli sicocxlis wyalia,
    iq RmerTi sicocxled Cqefs;
    mis dinebas RvTis ufloba,
    yvela adgilas Tan sdevs.
  3. is modis oqros quCaze,
    da ase gzas gviCvenebs;
    is RvTis bunebaSi moCqefs,
    Cvenc am gzaze rom davrCeT.
  4. masTan sicocxlis xec aris,
    RmerTs viT sakvebs gadmogvcems;
    mdinaris dinebis mier,
    vRebulobT xis siuxves.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    728. (ing. 985)

  1. im dRes Sen, o ufalo,
    gaanaTeb Cemgan;
    aRar dafaravs Tixis
    WurWeli RmerTis ganZs.
  2. im oqros WurWelidan
    naTobs dideba RvTis;
    mze saWiro ar aris,
    iq anaTebs RmerTi.
  3. qriste, rogorc Zviri qva
    morTavs qalaqs RmerTis;
    iaspisebr anaTebs,
    naTel didebaSi.
  4. im diad WurWelSi Cans
    didebis sinaTle,
    Tavisi sisavsiT is
    miwasac anaTebs.
  5. RmerTi didebas avlens
    axal qmnilebaSi;
    am didebis WurWeli
    kravis coli aris.
  6. oqros WurWliT tkbebian
    misi mxilvelebi;
    RmerTi gamoixata
    da gandidda kravSi.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    729.

  1. saocari saidumlo!
    Serwymulia kaci RmerTTan.
    RmerTi gaxda kaci, raTa
    kaci gamxdariyo RmerTi.
    Tavis saxlmSeneblobaSi:
    CauwvdomelSi, wmidaSi,
    umaRlesi aqvs mizani
    povebs riskenac iswrafvis.
  2. sisxliT _ xorciT Seimosa,
    gaxda pirveli RmerTkaci.
    mas surs, rom me viyo RmerTi
    sicocxliTa da bunebiT.
    RvTaebrioba RvTisaa!
    surs _ mqondes saxeba misi
    Cems saTnoebebSi, RmerTis
    gamovlindes Tvisebebi.
  3. axla marto aRar vcocxlob.
    axla vcocxlob RmerTTan erTad!
    samerTian RmerTSi, erTad,
    me vSendebi wmidanebTan,
    mis samyaroseul saxlad
    da sxeulad, organulad.
    Cven rom gvqondes, rogorc erT kacs _
    RmerTis gamoxatuleba.
  4. RmerTi da kaci, Cven da is _
    urTierTsamkvidrebeli.
    RmerTi da Cven, maradiul
    siyvarulSi myofi wyvili.
    ierusalimi aris
    yvela xedvis dasruleba!
    adamianurobidan
    RvTis dideba gabrwyindeba!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    730.

  1. RmerTo, Seni gadarCena
    Sens simarTles efuZneba;
    srulqmnilia organulad
    da iuridiuladac.
  2. samarTlebrivad gviyide,
    gadagvarCen organulad;
    simarTle aRsrulda Seni
    da Seni neba sruldeba.
  3. samarTlebrivad gavmarTldi,
    organulad SegierTdi;
    axla me viSvi RmerT-kacad,
    vwmidandebi da vaxldebi.
  4. Sens saxes davemsgavsebiT,
    metabolur gardasaxviT,
    sruli kacis zomas mivalT,
    erT sxeulad avSendebiT.
  5. gamosyiduli sxeuliT
    Zeni didebas mivaRwevT,
    Serwymuli urTierTsaxlad
    wmida qalaqze vimRerebT.

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    731. (ing. 986)

  1. qristem Cven gamogvisyida _
    o, saocari mxneli!
    man safasuriT gviyida _
    o, saocari mxsneli!

    mis:
    o, saocari mxsneli
    ieso aris CemTvis;
    o, saocari mxsneli
    ieso aris CemTvis!

    vaqeb mas gamwmend sisxlisTvis _
    o, saocari mxsneli!
    im sisxliT RmerTs Sevurigdi _
    o, saocari mxsneli!

    is me mwmends codvisgan sisxliT _
    o, saocari mxsneli!
    is marTavs da mefobs CemSi _
    o, saocari mxsneli!

  1. is CemSi yoveldRe cocxlobs _
    o, saocari mxsneli!
    erTgulad micavs Cems _

  2. gamarjvebis Zalas maZlevs _

  3. mas Cemi guli miveci _

    o, saocari mxsneli!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    732. (ing. 987)

  1. erT dRes, roca zecam is ganadida,
    erT dRes, roca codva pirquSobda,
    ieso qalwulisgan daibada _
    adamianTa Soris icxovra.

    mis:
    cocxals vuyvardi, sikvdiliT damixsna;
    damarxes _ waiRo Cemi codva;
    aRdga da saukunod gamamarTla _
    erT didebul dRes is dabrundeba!

  2. erT dRes is golgoTaze waiyvanes,
    erT dRes is jvarze mialursmes maT;
    gaitanja da moZulebul iqna;
    man xom Cveni codvebi itvirTa.
  3. erT dRes is datoves baRSi, saflavSi;
    erT dRes man tanjvisgan daisvena;
    angelozni mis samarxTan fxizlobdnen;
    ieso codvilTa imedia.
  4. erT dRes is samarxma veRar dafara,
    saflavis qva gadagorda erT dRes;
    Semdeg aRdga, sikvdilze gaimarjva,
    amaRlebaSi uflobs yvelaze.
  5. erT dRes sayviri mis mosvlas gvauwyebs,
    ca misi didebiT gabrwyindeba;
    is im dRes moiyvans Cems sayvarel xalxs;
    ieso Cemi didi mxsnelia!

    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    733. (ing. 988)

    mosiyvarule da
    wyalobiT savse
    Cven gamo itanja,
    wavida jvarze;
    is mokvda kacTaTvis _
    Cvens codvaTaTvis;
    ai, qriste mxsneli!
    ras izam misTvis?



    მთავარზე დაბრუნება

    734. (ing. 991)

  1. sixarulis uwyeba _
    ieso aris mxsneli!
    dae gaigon yvelgan _
    ieso aris mxsneli!
    axareT yvela miwas,
    miRma mTebis da zRvebis;
    `win~ _ ufalma gvibrZana;
    ieso aris mxsneli!
  2. dae qrolviT gavrceldes _
    ieso aris mxsneli!
    maS, vuamboT codvilebs _
    ieso aris mxsneli!
    zRvis kunZulni mRerodnen,
    okeanec gahyviris;
    miwa kvlav zeimobdes _
    ieso aris mxsneli.
  3. brZolis Semdeg imRereT _
